<div id="pgbrk" style="width: 100%; margin-left: 0px; text-indent: 0px; margin-right: 0px">
<div id="hdr">
<div style="text-align: right; width: 100%; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
&#xA0; <font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="font-weight: bold">Exhibit 99.1</font><br></font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px"><img src="tomz_ex991000.jpg"></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: center; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-weight: bold; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
TOMI ENVIRONMENTAL SOLUTIONS, INC. <font style="color: #000000">REPORTS</font></font></div>
<div style="text-align: center; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-weight: bold; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
FIRST QUARTER 2020 FINANCIAL RESULTS</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="color: #000000">
BEVERLY HILLS, CA, MAY 18, 2020 (BUSINESS WIRE) &#x2014;</font> TOMI
Environmental Solutions, Inc.<font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top">&#xAE;</font>
(&#x201C;TOMI&#x201D;) (OTCQB:TOMZ), is a global company specializing
in disinfection and decontamination, utilizing its premier Binary
Ionization Technology (BIT<font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000">&#x2122;</font>)
platform through its SteraMist<font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF">&#xAE;</font>
products - a hydrogen peroxide-based mist and fog composed of
ionized Hydrogen Peroxide (iHP<font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000">&#x2122;</font>),
<font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF">announced
its results for the first quarter of 2020.</font></font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">TOMI
Chief Executive Officer, Dr. Halden Shane stated, &#x201C;In the
beginning of 2020 the world saw a surge globally for disinfectants
and an enhanced level of clean to help prevent and mitigate the
spread of the SARS CoV-2 coronavirus, which has put TOMI and its
SteraMist<font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000">&#xAE;</font>
line of products front and center in the fight against this global
pandemic.</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">During
this pandemic our customer base has grown significantly. We remain
committed to keeping up with the increased demand and ensuring that
those fighting against the SARS CoV-2 virus are well-equipped with
our technology and solution. <font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF">We continue innovating
for a safer world by fighting coronavirus and other known and
emerging pathogens."</font></font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-weight: bold; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Financial Results for the Three Months Ended March 31, 2020
compared to March 31, 2019</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px;">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Total net revenue was $7,053,000 compared to $1,253,000,
representing an increase of $5,800,000, or 463%.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 48px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#x2013;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
SteraMist<font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000; font-family: Times New Roman">&#xAE;</font>
product-based revenues was $6,638,000 and $1,029,000, respectively,
representing an increase of $5,609,000 or 545%.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 48px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#x2013;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Service-based revenue was approximately $415,000 and $224,000,
respectively, representing a year over year increase of
85%.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 48px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#x2013;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Domestic revenue was $3,569,000 and $1,136,000, respectively,
representing an increase of $2,433,000, or 214%.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 48px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#x2013;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
International revenue was approximately $3,484,000 and $117,000,
respectively, representing an increase of $3,367,000 or
2,878%.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Gross margins were 63.6% compared to 60.6%. The higher gross profit
is attributable to the product mix in sales.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Income from operations was $2,659,000, compared to a Loss from
operations of ($868,000), representing an increase of $3,527,000,
or 406%.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Net Income was $2,619,000, or $0.02 on a per share basis compared
to a Net loss of ($935,000), or ($0.01) on a per share basis,
representing an increase of $3,554,000, or 380%.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Cash provided from operations of $3,316,000, compared to cash used
in operations of ($649,000).</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px;"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
EBIDTA was $2,831,000 compared to an adjusted net loss of
($691,000). A table reconciling EBITDA to the appropriate GAAP
measure is included with the Company's financial information
below.</font>&#xA0;<br></font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 24px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-weight: bold; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Balance sheet highlights as of March 31, 2020 and December 31,
2019</font></div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Cash and cash equivalents of approximately $3,756,000 and $897,000,
representing an increase of $2,859,000.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Working capital of $6,365,000 and ($1,266,000), representing an
increase of $7,631,000.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px;"><font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">Conversion
of $4,500,000 in convertible notes into 8,333,332 common
shares.</font>&#xA0;<br></font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">

</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row"><br></div>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-weight: bold; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Current Business Highlights To Date</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-weight: bold; font-style: italic; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Revenues</font></div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
First quarter revenue of $7,053,000 eclipsed total revenue

<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">

Customers</font></div>

<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Added one hundred and forty-one (141) customers to date in 2020,
representing a 571% increase over the same prior year
period.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">

<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Added thirty-one (31) new facilities in the hospital-healthcare
division to date in 2020, representing a 94% increase over the same
prior year period.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">

<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Added fifty-nine (59) new TSN providers to date in 2020,
representing a 1,833% increase over the same prior year period,
creating a total of 161 providers throughout 40 U.S. States and
Canada.</font></div>
</div>

Added twenty-nine (29) new customers to our Life Sciences customer
base, representing an increase of 263%.</font></div>

Added one (1) new Food Safety customer who purchased and

Business Highlights</font></div>

<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>

<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
As SteraMist<font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman">&#xAE;</font>

<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Expanded into the private aviation sector in Germany, multiple
market segments in Indonesia and hospital-healthcare, military and
homeland security in Singapore.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
New channels were opened as decontamination and disinfecting
processes are updated and implemented, including but not limited
to, fire departments, morgues, FAA, police departments, county and
state health departments, cruise ships, infectious disease research
facilities, military and ambulances.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Deployment of SteraMist<font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman">&#xAE;</font></font>
to be used around the world to decontaminate N95-equivalent
respirator masks, PAPRs, face shields, and other medical protective
equipment.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Binary Ionization Technology<font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman">&#xAE;</font></font>
(BIT<font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000; font-family: Times New Roman">&#x2122;</font></font>)
Solution qualified to meet the EPA Emerging Viral Pathogen Guidance
for Antimicrobial Pesticides with the SteraMist<font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman">&#xAE;</font></font></font>
Environment System for room fogging/misting against SARS-CoV-2, the
novel coronavirus that causes COVID-19.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-size: 13px">&#x25CF;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Registration of SteraMist<font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman">&#xAE;</font></font></font>
equipment and BIT<font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="color: #000000; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000; font-family: Times New Roman">&#x2122;</font></font></font>
solution with Chinese Center for Disease Control and Prevention
(China CDC).</font></div>

<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-weight: bold; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
TOMI<font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top">&#x2122;</font> Environmental
Solutions, Inc.: Innovating for a safer world<font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top">&#xAE;</font></font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="color: #000000">
TOMI</font><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000">&#x2122;&#xA0;</font><font style="color: #000000">Environmental
Solutions, Inc. (OTCQB:</font><font style="text-decoration: underline; color: #954F72">TOMZ</font><font style="color: #000000">)
is a global decontamination and infection prevention company,
providing environmental solutions for indoor surface disinfection
through the manufacturing, sales and licensing of its premier
Binary Ionization Technology</font><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000">&#xAE;</font><font style="color: #000000">&#xA0;(BIT</font><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000">&#x2122;</font><font style="color: #000000">)
platform</font><font style="color: #000000">. Invented under a
defense grant in association with the Defense Advanced Research
Projects Agency (DARPA) of the U.S. Department of Defense,
BIT</font><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000">&#x2122;</font><font style="color: #000000">&#xA0;solution
utilizes a low percentage Hydrogen Peroxide as its only active
ingredient to produce a fog of ionized Hydrogen Peroxide
(iHP</font><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000">&#x2122;</font><font style="color: #000000">).
Represented by the SteraMist</font><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000">&#xAE;</font>
<font style="color: #000000">brand of products,
iHP</font><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000">&#x2122;</font>
<font style="color: #000000">produces a germ-killing aerosol that
works like a visual non-caustic gas.</font></font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
TOMI&#xA0;products are designed to service a broad spectrum of
commercial structures, including, but not limited to, hospitals and
medical facilities, cruise ships, office buildings, hotel and motel
rooms, schools, restaurants, meat and produce processing
facilities, military barracks, police and fire departments, and
athletic facilities.&#xA0;TOMI&#xA0;products and services have also
been used in single-family homes and multi-unit
residences.</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">

TOMI</font><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #000000">&#xA0;</font><font style="color: #000000">develops

<font style="font-weight: bold; color: #000000; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Use of Non-GAAP Measures</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="color: #000000; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
The Company has supplemented its reported GAAP (generally accepted
accounting principles) financial information with non-GAAP
measures. EBITDA and Adjusted Net Loss was derived by taking
earnings before interest expense (net), taxes, depreciation and
amortization. The presentation of this additional information is
not meant to be considered in isolation or as a substitute for
results prepared in accordance with U.S. GAAP. The Company believes
this non-GAAP measure is useful to investors as it provides a basis
for evaluating the Company's operating results in the ordinary
course of its operations. This non-GAAP measure is not based on any
comprehensive set of accounting rules or principles. The Company
believes that non-GAAP measures have limitations in that they do
not reflect all of the amounts associated with its results of
operations as determined in accordance with U.S. GAAP and that
these measures should only be used to evaluate the Company's
results of operations in conjunction with, and not in lieu of, the
corresponding GAAP measures. EBITDA are reconciled in the tables
above to the most directly comparable measure as reported in
accordance with GAAP.</font></div>
